<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Public_transit">Public transit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Public transit">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PalmTran" title="PalmTran">PalmTran</a> provides bus service throughout Palm Beach county.</li>
</ul>
<p>Tri-Rail provides Commuter Rail service with stops from Miami and Broward Counties</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Seaport">Seaport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Seaport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Palm_Beach" title="Port of Palm Beach">Port of Palm Beach</a> is located in Riviera Beach, where <a href="/wiki/Celebration_Cruise_Line" title="Celebration Cruise Line">Celebration Cruise Line</a> operates 2-day cruises to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">Bahamas</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trails">Trails</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Trails">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Lake_Okeechobee_Scenic_Trail" title="Lake Okeechobee Scenic Trail">Lake Okeechobee Scenic Trail</a>, a segment of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_National_Scenic_Trail" title="Florida National Scenic Trail">Florida National Scenic Trail</a>, passes through the County.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Primary_and_secondary_schools">Primary and secondary schools</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Primary and secondary schools">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>All of Palm Beach County is served by the <a href="/wiki/School_District_of_Palm_Beach_County" title="School District of Palm Beach County">School District of Palm Beach County</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup> As of 2006, it was the 4th largest school district in Florida and the <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_largest_school_districts_in_the_United_States_by_enrollment" title="List of the largest school districts in the United States by enrollment">11th largest</a> school district in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. As of August 2006, the district operated 164 schools, including 25 high schools, and, as of July 22, 2006 had an additional 33 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charter_schools" title="Charter schools">charter schools</a>, with seven more scheduled to open in August 2006.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup> Newsweek listed three Palm Beach County high schools in the top 50 schools in the list 1200 Top U.S. Schools - <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Community_High_School" title="Atlantic Community High School">Atlantic Community High School</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suncoast_High_School" title="Suncoast High School">Suncoast High School</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alexander_Dreyfoos_School_of_the_Arts" title="Alexander Dreyfoos School of the Arts">Alexander Dreyfoos School of the Arts</a>, all public <a href="/wiki/Magnet_school" title="Magnet school">magnet schools</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup> Private schools in the county include <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=American_Heritage_School_(Delray_Beach,_Florida)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="American Heritage School (Delray Beach, Florida) (page does not exist)">American Heritage School</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_Newman_High_School_(West_Palm_Beach,_Florida)" title="Cardinal Newman High School (West Palm Beach, Florida)">Cardinal Newman High School</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jupiter_Christian_School" title="Jupiter Christian School">Jupiter Christian School</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_King%27s_Academy_(West_Palm_Beach,_Florida)" title="The King's Academy (West Palm Beach, Florida)">The King's Academy</a>, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_Benjamin_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The Benjamin School (page does not exist)">The Benjamin School</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oxbridge_Academy" title="Oxbridge Academy">Oxbridge Academy</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pope_John_Paul_II_High_School_(Florida)" title="Pope John Paul II High School (Florida)">Pope John Paul II High School</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Andrew%27s_School_(Boca_Raton,_Florida)" title="Saint Andrew's School (Boca Raton, Florida)">St Andrew's School</a> and <a href="/wiki/Weinbaum_Yeshiva_High_School" title="Weinbaum Yeshiva High School">Weinbaum Yeshiva High School</a>.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Public_libraries">Public libraries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Public libraries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_County_Library_System" title="Palm Beach County Library System">Palm Beach County Library System</a> operates public libraries, the main one being the Main Library on Summit Blvd.</p>
<p>The city of <a href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach,_Florida" title="West Palm Beach, Florida">West Palm Beach</a> operates the <a href="/wiki/Mandel_Public_Library_of_West_Palm_Beach" title="Mandel Public Library of West Palm Beach">Mandel Public Library of West Palm Beach</a> for its residents. Other cities, such as <a href="/wiki/Boca_Raton,_Florida" title="Boca Raton, Florida">Boca Raton</a> and several others, also operate public libraries for their residents</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/St._Louis_Cardinals" title="St. Louis Cardinals">St. Louis Cardinals</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Marlins" title="Miami Marlins">Miami Marlins</a> conduct their <a href="/wiki/Spring_training" title="Spring training">spring training</a> at <a href="/wiki/Roger_Dean_Stadium" title="Roger Dean Stadium">Roger Dean Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jupiter,_Florida" title="Jupiter, Florida">Jupiter</a>. Two teams in the Class A-Advanced <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_League" title="Florida State League">Florida State League</a> also play their home games at Roger Dean Stadium: the <a href="/wiki/Jupiter_Hammerheads" title="Jupiter Hammerheads">Jupiter Hammerheads</a>, an affiliate of the Miami Marlins, and the <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_Cardinals" title="Palm Beach Cardinals">Palm Beach Cardinals</a>, an affiliate of the St. Louis Cardinals.</p>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Ballpark_of_The_Palm_Beaches" title="The Ballpark of The Palm Beaches">The Ballpark of The Palm Beaches</a>, opened in February 2017 in <a href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach,_Florida" title="West Palm Beach, Florida">West Palm Beach</a>, accommodates both the <a href="/wiki/Washington_Nationals" title="Washington Nationals">Washington Nationals</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Houston_Astros" title="Houston Astros">Houston Astros</a> for spring training.</p>
<p>Prior to the construction of Roger Dean Stadium, the <a href="/wiki/Montreal_Expos" title="Montreal Expos">Montreal Expos</a> and <a href="/wiki/Atlanta_Braves" title="Atlanta Braves">Atlanta Braves</a> held their spring training at <a href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach_Municipal_Stadium" title="West Palm Beach Municipal Stadium">Municipal Stadium</a> in West Palm Beach. The <a href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach_Expos" title="West Palm Beach Expos">West Palm Beach Expos</a>, a Single-A affiliate of the Montreal Expos, also played their games there.</p>
<p>Also popular are the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_Atlantic_University_Owls" title="Florida Atlantic University Owls">Florida Atlantic Owls</a>, an NCAA Division I school that participates in <a href="/wiki/Conference_USA" title="Conference USA">Conference USA</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Florida_Atlantic_Owls_football" title="Florida Atlantic Owls football">FAU football</a> team play at <a href="/wiki/FAU_Stadium" title="FAU Stadium">FAU Stadium</a>, and averaged 14,552 fans during the 2013 season.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Florida_Atlantic_Owls_men%27s_basketball" title="Florida Atlantic Owls men's basketball">FAU basketball</a> team plays at <a href="/wiki/FAU_Arena" title="FAU Arena">FAU Arena</a>, and averaged 1,346 fans during the 2013–14 season.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_Imperials" title="Palm Beach Imperials">Palm Beach Imperials</a> are an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_Basketball_Association_(21st_century)" title="American Basketball Association (21st century)">American Basketball Association</a> 2006 expansion franchise.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Communities">Communities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Communities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1000" height="320" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg/400px-Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg/600px-Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg/800px-Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg.png 2x" width="400"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cities_of_Palm_Beach_County.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Map of incorporated cities.\</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="679" data-file-width="1024" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg/220px-BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg/330px-BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg/440px-BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:BoyntonBeach%26BocaRatonFromTheISS.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Southeastern Palm Beach County (from Boca Raton to Boynton Beach), seen from the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The largest city and <a href="/wiki/County_seat" title="County seat">county seat</a> is <a href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach,_Florida" title="West Palm Beach, Florida">West Palm Beach</a>, with an estimated population of over 105,000. Additionally, the approximate urban population is 250,000, when including adjacent unincorporated neighborhoods. <a href="/wiki/Boca_Raton,_Florida" title="Boca Raton, Florida">Boca Raton</a> (South County), is the second largest, having a population approaching 90,000. <a href="/wiki/Boynton_Beach,_Florida" title="Boynton Beach, Florida">Boynton Beach</a> (South County), is the third largest city, with a population nearing 70,000 residents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_89-0"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-89">[89]</a></sup></p>
<p>The county has 38 municipalities in total. The municipalities are numbered corresponding to the attached image. Municipality populations are based on the <a href="/wiki/2010_United_States_Census" title="2010 United States Census">2010 Census</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_census-designated_places">Former census-designated places</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palm_Beach_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Former census-designated places">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Several unincorporated parts of Palm Beach County were listed as census-designated places for the <a href="/wiki/2000_United_States_Census" title="2000 United States Census">2000 census</a> but were not listed for the <a href="/wiki/2010_United_States_Census" title="2010 United States Census">2010 census</a>:</p>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 15em; -webkit-column-width: 15em; column-width: 15em;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belle_Glade_Camp,_Florida" title="Belle Glade Camp, Florida">Belle Glade Camp</a> (l)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boca_Del_Mar,_Florida" title="Boca Del Mar, Florida">Boca Del Mar</a> (c)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boca_Pointe,_Florida" title="Boca Pointe, Florida">Boca Pointe</a> (a)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cypress_Lakes,_Florida" title="Cypress Lakes, Florida">Cypress Lakes</a> (w)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dunes_Road,_Florida" title="Dunes Road, Florida">Dunes Road</a> (cc)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fremd_Village-Padgett_Island,_Florida" title="Fremd Village-Padgett Island, Florida">Fremd Village-Padgett Island</a> (aa)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Golden_Lakes,_Florida" title="Golden Lakes, Florida">Golden Lakes</a> (r)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hamptons_at_Boca_Raton,_Florida" title="Hamptons at Boca Raton, Florida">Hamptons at Boca Raton</a> (e)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/High_Point,_Palm_Beach_County,_Florida" title="High Point, Palm Beach County, Florida">High Point</a> (i)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kings_Point,_Florida" title="Kings Point, Florida">Kings Point</a> (g)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lake_Worth_Corridor,_Florida" title="Lake Worth Corridor, Florida">Lake Worth Corridor</a> (k)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lakeside_Green,_Florida" title="Lakeside Green, Florida">Lakeside Green</a> (x)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mission_Bay,_Florida" title="Mission Bay, Florida">Mission Bay</a> (d)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sandalfoot_Cove,_Florida" title="Sandalfoot Cove, Florida">Sandalfoot Cove</a> (b)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Villages_of_Oriole,_Florida" title="Villages of Oriole, Florida">Villages of Oriole</a> (h)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Whisper_Walk,_Florida" title="Whisper Walk, Florida">Whisper Walk</a> (f)</li>
</ul>
</div>
